<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-167">使用、复制和分发的条款和条件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-167">TERMS AND CONDITIONS FOR USE, REPRODUCTION, AND DISTRIBUTION</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-168">限定.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-168">Definitions.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-169">"许可证" 是指本文档的第1和第9节所定义的使用、复制和分发的条款和条件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-169">"License" shall mean the terms and conditions for use, reproduction, and distribution as defined by Sections 1 through 9 of this document.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-170">"许可方" 是指由授予许可证的版权所有所有者授权的版权所有者或实体。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-170">"Licensor" shall mean the copyright owner or entity authorized by the copyright owner that is granting the License.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-171">"法人" 是指使用该实体的公共控制和控制、控制的作用图元和所有其他实体的联合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-171">"Legal Entity" shall mean the union of the acting entity and all other entities that control, are controlled by, or are under common control with that entity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-172">出于此定义的目的，"控制" 是指（i）电源、直接或间接地引发此类实体的方向或管理（无论是按合同还是以其他方式）或（ii）所有权的50% （50%）或（iii）对此类实体拥有有益所有权的多个未完成的共享或（iii）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-172">For the purposes of this definition, "control" means (i) the power, direct or indirect, to cause the direction or management of such entity, whether by contract or otherwise, or (ii) ownership of fifty percent (50%) or more of the outstanding shares, or (iii) beneficial ownership of such entity.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-173">"您" （或 "您的"）是指由该许可证授予的个人或法律实体的权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-173">"You" (or "Your") shall mean an individual or Legal Entity exercising permissions granted by this License.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-174">"源" 表单应表示进行修改的首选表单，包括但不限于软件源代码、文档源和配置文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-174">"Source" form shall mean the preferred form for making modifications, including but not limited to software source code, documentation source, and configuration files.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-175">"对象" 表单是指从机械转换或源表单转换中产生的任何表单，包括但不限于已编译的对象代码、生成的文档以及转换为其他媒体类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-175">"Object" form shall mean any form resulting from mechanical transformation or translation of a Source form, including but not limited to compiled object code, generated documentation, and conversions to other media types.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-176">"工时" 是指在许可证下提供的 authorship （在源表单或对象表单中）的工作，如中所包含或附加到工作中的版权声明所指示（以下附录中提供了示例）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-176">"Work" shall mean the work of authorship, whether in Source or Object form, made available under the License, as indicated by a copyright notice that is included in or attached to the work (an example is provided in the Appendix below).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-177">"衍生品" 是指在源或对象窗体中基于（或衍生自）工作，以及编辑修订、批注、elaborations 或其他修改都代表 authorship 的原始工作的任何工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-177">"Derivative Works" shall mean any work, whether in Source or Object form, that is based on (or derived from) the Work and for which the editorial revisions, annotations, elaborations, or other modifications represent, as a whole, an original work of authorship.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-178">出于此许可证的目的，衍生品不应包括可从其分离的工作，或者仅链接（或按名称绑定）到的接口，工作和衍生工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-178">For the purposes of this License, Derivative Works shall not include works that remain separable from, or merely link (or bind by name) to the interfaces of, the Work and Derivative Works thereof.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-179">"贡献" 是指 authorship 的任何工作，包括原始版本的工作，以及对该工作或衍生作品的任何修改或补充，这些都是有意提交到许可方以供版权所有者在工作中包含的，或者由授权在代表版权所有者提交的个人或法律实体。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-179">"Contribution" shall mean any work of authorship, including the original version of the Work and any modifications or additions to that Work or Derivative Works thereof, that is intentionally submitted to Licensor for inclusion in the Work by the copyright owner or by an individual or Legal Entity authorized to submit on behalf of the copyright owner.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-180">对于此定义，"已提交" 表示发送给许可方或其代表的任何形式的电子、口头或书面通信，包括但不限于电子邮件列表、源代码控制系统和颁发或代表的用于讨论和改进工作的许可方的跟踪系统，但不包括被 conspicuously 标记或指定为版权所有者写入的内容为 "不是投稿" 的通信。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-180">For the purposes of this definition, "submitted" means any form of electronic, verbal, or written communication sent to the Licensor or its representatives, including but not limited to communication on electronic mailing lists, source code control systems, and issue tracking systems that are managed by, or on behalf of, the Licensor for the purpose of discussing and improving the Work, but excluding communication that is conspicuously marked or otherwise designated in writing by the copyright owner as "Not a Contribution."</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-181">"投稿人" 是指许可方和任何个人或法人代表许可方接收到的内容，随后合并在工作中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-181">"Contributor" shall mean Licensor and any individual or Legal Entity on behalf of whom a Contribution has been received by Licensor and subsequently incorporated within the Work.</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-182">授予版权许可证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-182">Grant of Copyright License.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-183">根据此许可证的条款和条件，每个参与者特此授予您一种永久的、全球、非独占、免费、免版税、不可撤销的版权许可证，以重现、准备好的衍生作品、公开发布在源或对象窗体中执行、再颁发和分发工作以及此类派生作品。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-183">Subject to the terms and conditions of this License, each Contributor hereby grants to You a perpetual, worldwide, non-exclusive, no-charge, royalty-free, irrevocable copyright license to reproduce, prepare Derivative Works of, publicly display, publicly perform, sublicense, and distribute the Work and such Derivative Works in Source or Object form.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-189">您必须为工作或衍生作品的任何其他收件人提供此许可证的副本;并</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-189">You must give any other recipients of the Work or Derivative Works a copy of this License; and</span></span>

## <a name="caseless-v0120"></a>[<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-302">caseless v 0.12。0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-302">caseless v0.12.0</span></span>](https://github.com/request/caseless/blob/master/LICENSE)

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-303">Apache 许可证版本2.0，2004 http://www.apache.org/licenses/年1月的使用、复制和分发的条款和条件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-303">Apache License Version 2.0, January 2004 http://www.apache.org/licenses/ TERMS AND CONDITIONS FOR USE, REPRODUCTION, AND DISTRIBUTION</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-304">限定.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-304">Definitions.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-305">"许可证" 是指本文档的第1和第9节所定义的使用、复制和分发的条款和条件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-305">"License" shall mean the terms and conditions for use, reproduction, and distribution as defined by Sections 1 through 9 of this document.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-306">"许可方" 是指由授予许可证的版权所有所有者授权的版权所有者或实体。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-306">"Licensor" shall mean the copyright owner or entity authorized by the copyright owner that is granting the License.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-307">"法人" 是指使用该实体的公共控制和控制、控制的作用图元和所有其他实体的联合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-307">"Legal Entity" shall mean the union of the acting entity and all other entities that control, are controlled by, or are under common control with that entity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-308">出于此定义的目的，"控制" 是指（i）电源、直接或间接地引发此类实体的方向或管理（无论是按合同还是以其他方式）或（ii）所有权的50% （50%）或（iii）对此类实体拥有有益所有权的多个未完成的共享或（iii）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-308">For the purposes of this definition, "control" means (i) the power, direct or indirect, to cause the direction or management of such entity, whether by contract or otherwise, or (ii) ownership of fifty percent (50%) or more of the outstanding shares, or (iii) beneficial ownership of such entity.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-309">"您" （或 "您的"）是指由该许可证授予的个人或法律实体的权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-309">"You" (or "Your") shall mean an individual or Legal Entity exercising permissions granted by this License.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-310">"源" 表单应表示进行修改的首选表单，包括但不限于软件源代码、文档源和配置文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-310">"Source" form shall mean the preferred form for making modifications, including but not limited to software source code, documentation source, and configuration files.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-311">"对象" 表单是指从机械转换或源表单转换中产生的任何表单，包括但不限于已编译的对象代码、生成的文档以及转换为其他媒体类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-311">"Object" form shall mean any form resulting from mechanical transformation or translation of a Source form, including but not limited to compiled object code, generated documentation, and conversions to other media types.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-312">"工时" 是指在许可证下提供的 authorship （在源表单或对象表单中）的工作，如中所包含或附加到工作中的版权声明所指示（以下附录中提供了示例）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-312">"Work" shall mean the work of authorship, whether in Source or Object form, made available under the License, as indicated by a copyright notice that is included in or attached to the work (an example is provided in the Appendix below).</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-313">"衍生品" 是指在源或对象窗体中基于（或衍生自）工作，以及编辑修订、批注、elaborations 或其他修改都代表 authorship 的原始工作的任何工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-313">"Derivative Works" shall mean any work, whether in Source or Object form, that is based on (or derived from) the Work and for which the editorial revisions, annotations, elaborations, or other modifications represent, as a whole, an original work of authorship.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-314">出于此许可证的目的，衍生品不应包括可从其分离的工作，或者仅链接（或按名称绑定）到的接口，工作和衍生工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-314">For the purposes of this License, Derivative Works shall not include works that remain separable from, or merely link (or bind by name) to the interfaces of, the Work and Derivative Works thereof.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-315">"贡献" 是指 authorship 的任何工作，包括原始版本的工作，以及对该工作或衍生作品的任何修改或补充，这些都是有意提交到许可方以供版权所有者在工作中包含的，或者由授权在代表版权所有者提交的个人或法律实体。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-315">"Contribution" shall mean any work of authorship, including the original version of the Work and any modifications or additions to that Work or Derivative Works thereof, that is intentionally submitted to Licensor for inclusion in the Work by the copyright owner or by an individual or Legal Entity authorized to submit on behalf of the copyright owner.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-316">对于此定义，"已提交" 表示发送给许可方或其代表的任何形式的电子、口头或书面通信，包括但不限于电子邮件列表、源代码控制系统和颁发或代表的用于讨论和改进工作的许可方的跟踪系统，但不包括被 conspicuously 标记或指定为版权所有者写入的内容为 "不是投稿" 的通信。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-316">For the purposes of this definition, "submitted" means any form of electronic, verbal, or written communication sent to the Licensor or its representatives, including but not limited to communication on electronic mailing lists, source code control systems, and issue tracking systems that are managed by, or on behalf of, the Licensor for the purpose of discussing and improving the Work, but excluding communication that is conspicuously marked or otherwise designated in writing by the copyright owner as "Not a Contribution."</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-317">"投稿人" 是指许可方和任何个人或法人代表许可方接收到的内容，随后合并在工作中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-317">"Contributor" shall mean Licensor and any individual or Legal Entity on behalf of whom a Contribution has been received by Licensor and subsequently incorporated within the Work.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-318">授予版权许可证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-318">Grant of Copyright License.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-319">根据此许可证的条款和条件，每个参与者特此授予您一种永久的、全球、非独占、免费、免版税、不可撤销的版权许可证，以重现、准备好的衍生作品、公开发布在源或对象窗体中执行、再颁发和分发工作以及此类派生作品。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-319">Subject to the terms and conditions of this License, each Contributor hereby grants to You a perpetual, worldwide, non-exclusive, no-charge, royalty-free, irrevocable copyright license to reproduce, prepare Derivative Works of, publicly display, publicly perform, sublicense, and distribute the Work and such Derivative Works in Source or Object form.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-320">授予专利许可证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-320">Grant of Patent License.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-321">根据此许可证的条款和条件，每个参与者特此授予您一个永久的、全球性的、非独占的、免费、免版税、不可撤销的永久性许可证（除非本部分中所述）专利许可证进行制作、使用、提供销售、销售、导入并以其他方式传输工作，此类许可证仅适用于这些投稿人许可的那些专利声明，这些专利声明一定是由这些参与者提供的 infringed，也可以是其与此类工作的贡献的组合（s）。提交了 #a0 个内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-321">Subject to the terms and conditions of this License, each Contributor hereby grants to You a perpetual, worldwide, non-exclusive, no-charge, royalty-free, irrevocable (except as stated in this section) patent license to make, have made, use, offer to sell, sell, import, and otherwise transfer the Work, where such license applies only to those patent claims licensable by such Contributor that are necessarily infringed by their Contribution(s) alone or by combination of their Contribution(s) with the Work to which such Contribution(s) was submitted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-322">如果您对任何实体（包括跨声明或 lawsuit 中的 counterclaim）进行专利诉讼，宣称中加入的工作或贡献构成了直接或 contributory 的专利侵权行为，以及任何专利许可证根据此许可证向你授予此工作的许可证应在存档此类诉讼时终止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-322">If You institute patent litigation against any entity (including a cross-claim or counterclaim in a lawsuit) alleging that the Work or a Contribution incorporated within the Work constitutes direct or contributory patent infringement, then any patent licenses granted to You under this License for that Work shall terminate as of the date such litigation is filed.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-323">重新.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-323">Redistribution.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-324">如果满足以下条件，则可以复制和分发任何媒体（无论是否有修改）中的工作或派生作品的副本。在源或对象窗体中，只要满足以下条件即可：您必须为工作或衍生产品提供任何其他收件人此许可证的副本是否有效;并且，您必须让任何修改过的文件携带突出的声明，表明您已更改文件;您必须在所分发的任何派生作品的源表单中，保留工作源形式的所有版权、专利、商标和归属声明，不包括那些不与衍生作品的任何部分相关的声明;如果工作中包含 "通知" 文本文件作为其分布的一部分，则您分发的任何派生作品都必须包含此通知文件中包含的归属声明的可读副本，不包括那些不属于任何部分的声明导数在以下位置中至少有一个：在作为导数工作的一部分分发的通知文本文件中;在源表单或文档中，如果随衍生作品一起提供，则为或者，在导数的工作所生成的显示中，如果在通常显示此类第三方通知的任何位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-324">You may reproduce and distribute copies of the Work or Derivative Works thereof in any medium, with or without modifications, and in Source or Object form, provided that You meet the following conditions: You must give any other recipients of the Work or Derivative Works a copy of this License; and You must cause any modified files to carry prominent notices stating that You changed the files; and You must retain, in the Source form of any Derivative Works that You distribute, all copyright, patent, trademark, and attribution notices from the Source form of the Work, excluding those notices that do not pertain to any part of the Derivative Works; and If the Work includes a "NOTICE" text file as part of its distribution, then any Derivative Works that You distribute must include a readable copy of the attribution notices contained within such NOTICE file, excluding those notices that do not pertain to any part of the Derivative Works, in at least one of the following places: within a NOTICE text file distributed as part of the Derivative Works;    <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-468">使用、复制和分发的条款和条件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-468">TERMS AND CONDITIONS FOR USE, REPRODUCTION, AND DISTRIBUTION</span></span>

   1. <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-469">限定.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-469">Definitions.</span></span>

      <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-470">"许可证" 是指本文档的第1和第9节所定义的使用、复制和分发的条款和条件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-470">"License" shall mean the terms and conditions for use, reproduction, and distribution as defined by Sections 1 through 9 of this document.</span></span>

      <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-471">"许可方" 是指由授予许可证的版权所有所有者授权的版权所有者或实体。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-471">"Licensor" shall mean the copyright owner or entity authorized by the copyright owner that is granting the License.</span></span>

      <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-472">"法人" 是指使用该实体的公共控制和控制、控制的作用图元和所有其他实体的联合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-472">"Legal Entity" shall mean the union of the acting entity and all other entities that control, are controlled by, or are under common control with that entity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-473">出于此定义的目的，"控制" 是指（i）电源、直接或间接地引发此类实体的方向或管理（无论是按合同还是以其他方式）或（ii）所有权的50% （50%）或（iii）对此类实体拥有有益所有权的多个未完成的共享或（iii）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-473">For the purposes of this definition, "control" means (i) the power, direct or indirect, to cause the direction or management of such entity, whether by contract or otherwise, or (ii) ownership of fifty percent (50%) or more of the outstanding shares, or (iii) beneficial ownership of such entity.</span></span>

      <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-474">"您" （或 "您的"）是指由该许可证授予的个人或法律实体的权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-474">"You" (or "Your") shall mean an individual or Legal Entity exercising permissions granted by this License.</span></span>

      <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-475">"源" 表单应表示进行修改的首选表单，包括但不限于软件源代码、文档源和配置文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-475">"Source" form shall mean the preferred form for making modifications, including but not limited to software source code, documentation source, and configuration files.</span></span>

      <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-476">"对象" 表单是指从机械转换或源表单转换中产生的任何表单，包括但不限于已编译的对象代码、生成的文档以及转换为其他媒体类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-476">"Object" form shall mean any form resulting from mechanical transformation or translation of a Source form, including but not limited to compiled object code, generated documentation, and conversions to other media types.</span></span>

      <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-477">"工时" 是指在许可证下提供的 authorship （在源表单或对象表单中）的工作，如中所包含或附加到工作中的版权声明所指示（以下附录中提供了示例）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-477">"Work" shall mean the work of authorship, whether in Source or Object form, made available under the License, as indicated by a copyright notice that is included in or attached to the work (an example is provided in the Appendix below).</span></span>

      <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-478">"衍生品" 是指在源或对象窗体中基于（或衍生自）工作，以及编辑修订、批注、elaborations 或其他修改都代表 authorship 的原始工作的任何工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-478">"Derivative Works" shall mean any work, whether in Source or Object form, that is based on (or derived from) the Work and for which the editorial revisions, annotations, elaborations, or other modifications represent, as a whole, an original work of authorship.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-479">出于此许可证的目的，衍生品不应包括可从其分离的工作，或者仅链接（或按名称绑定）到的接口，工作和衍生工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-479">For the purposes of this License, Derivative Works shall not include works that remain separable from, or merely link (or bind by name) to the interfaces of, the Work and Derivative Works thereof.</span></span>

      <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-480">"贡献" 是指 authorship 的任何工作，包括原始版本的工作，以及对该工作或衍生作品的任何修改或补充，这些都是有意提交到许可方以供版权所有者在工作中包含的，或者由授权在代表版权所有者提交的个人或法律实体。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-480">"Contribution" shall mean any work of authorship, including the original version of the Work and any modifications or additions to that Work or Derivative Works thereof, that is intentionally submitted to Licensor for inclusion in the Work by the copyright owner or by an individual or Legal Entity authorized to submit on behalf of the copyright owner.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-481">对于此定义，"已提交" 表示发送给许可方或其代表的任何形式的电子、口头或书面通信，包括但不限于电子邮件列表、源代码控制系统和颁发或代表的用于讨论和改进工作的许可方的跟踪系统，但不包括被 conspicuously 标记或指定为版权所有者写入的内容为 "不是投稿" 的通信。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-481">For the purposes of this definition, "submitted" means any form of electronic, verbal, or written communication sent to the Licensor or its representatives, including but not limited to communication on electronic mailing lists, source code control systems, and issue tracking systems that are managed by, or on behalf of, the Licensor for the purpose of discussing and improving the Work, but excluding communication that is conspicuously marked or otherwise designated in writing by the copyright owner as "Not a Contribution."</span></span>

      <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-482">"投稿人" 是指许可方和任何个人或法人代表许可方接收到的内容，随后合并在工作中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-482">"Contributor" shall mean Licensor and any individual or Legal Entity on behalf of whom a Contribution has been received by Licensor and subsequently incorporated within the Work.</span></span>

   2. <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-483">授予版权许可证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-483">Grant of Copyright License.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-484">根据此许可证的条款和条件，每个参与者特此授予您一种永久的、全球、非独占、免费、免版税、不可撤销的版权许可证，以重现、准备好的衍生作品、公开发布在源或对象窗体中执行、再颁发和分发工作以及此类派生作品。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-484">Subject to the terms and conditions of this License, each Contributor hereby grants to You a perpetual, worldwide, non-exclusive, no-charge, royalty-free, irrevocable copyright license to reproduce, prepare Derivative Works of, publicly display, publicly perform, sublicense, and distribute the Work and such Derivative Works in Source or Object form.</span></span>

   3. <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-485">授予专利许可证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-485">Grant of Patent License.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-486">根据此许可证的条款和条件，每个参与者特此授予您一个永久的、全球性的、非独占的、免费、免版税、不可撤销的永久性许可证（除非本部分中所述）专利许可证进行制作、使用、提供销售、销售、导入并以其他方式传输工作，此类许可证仅适用于这些投稿人许可的那些专利声明，这些专利声明一定是由这些参与者提供的 infringed，也可以是其与此类工作的贡献的组合（s）。提交了 #a0 个内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-486">Subject to the terms and conditions of this License, each Contributor hereby grants to You a perpetual, worldwide, non-exclusive, no-charge, royalty-free, irrevocable (except as stated in this section) patent license to make, have made, use, offer to sell, sell, import, and otherwise transfer the Work, where such license applies only to those patent claims licensable by such Contributor that are necessarily infringed by their Contribution(s) alone or by combination of their Contribution(s) with the Work to which such Contribution(s) was submitted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-487">如果您对任何实体（包括跨声明或 lawsuit 中的 counterclaim）进行专利诉讼，宣称中加入的工作或贡献构成了直接或 contributory 的专利侵权行为，以及任何专利许可证根据此许可证向你授予此工作的许可证应在存档此类诉讼时终止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-487">If You institute patent litigation against any entity (including a cross-claim or counterclaim in a lawsuit) alleging that the Work or a Contribution incorporated within the Work constitutes direct or contributory patent infringement, then any patent licenses granted to You under this License for that Work shall terminate as of the date such litigation is filed.</span></span>

   4. <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-488">重新.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-488">Redistribution.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-489">如果满足以下条件，则可以复制和分发任何媒体（无论是否有修改）中的工作或派生作品的副本。在源或对象窗体中，只要满足以下条件即可：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-489">You may reproduce and distribute copies of the Work or Derivative Works thereof in any medium, with or without modifications, and in Source or Object form, provided that You meet the following conditions:</span></span>

      <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-490">（a）您必须为工作或衍生作品的任何其他收件人提供此许可证的副本;并</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-490">(a) You must give any other recipients of the Work or     Derivative Works a copy of this License; and</span></span>

      <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-491">（b）您必须导致任何已修改的文件携带突出的说明，表明您已更改这些文件;并</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-491">(b) You must cause any modified files to carry prominent notices     stating that You changed the files; and</span></span>

      <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-492">（c）您必须在所分发的任何衍生作品的源表单中保留所有版权、专利、商标和归属声明，不包括那些不与衍生作品的任何部分相关的声明;并</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-492">(c) You must retain, in the Source form of any Derivative Works     that You distribute, all copyright, patent, trademark, and     attribution notices from the Source form of the Work,     excluding those notices that do not pertain to any part of     the Derivative Works; and</span></span>

      <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-493">（d）如果工作包含作为其分布的一部分的 "通知" 文本文件，则您所分发的任何派生作品都必须包含此通知文件中包含的归属声明的可读副本，不包括那些不属于任何部分的声明导数在以下位置中至少有一个：在作为导数工作的一部分分发的通知文本文件中;在源表单或文档中，如果随衍生作品一起提供，则为或者，在导数的工作所生成的显示中，如果在通常显示此类第三方通知的任何位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-493">(d) If the Work includes a "NOTICE" text file as part of its distribution, then any Derivative Works that You distribute must include a readable copy of the attribution notices contained within such NOTICE file, excluding those notices that do not pertain to any part of the Derivative Works, in at least one of the following places: within a NOTICE text file distributed as part of the Derivative Works; within the Source form or documentation, if provided along with the Derivative Works; or, within a display generated by the Derivative Works, if and wherever such third-party notices normally appear.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-494">通知文件的内容仅用于提供信息，不会修改许可证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-494">The contents of the NOTICE file are for informational purposes only and do not modify the License.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-495">您可以在所分发的派生作品中添加自己的归属声明，也可以在工作中添加声明文本的补充或作为说明，前提是无法将此类附加归属声明解释为修改许可证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-495">You may add Your own attribution notices within Derivative Works that You distribute, alongside or as an addendum to the NOTICE text from the Work, provided that such additional attribution notices cannot be construed as modifying the License.</span></span>

      <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-496">您可以向所做的修改中添加自己的版权声明，并提供其他或不同的许可条款和条件，以供使用、复制或分发所做的修改，或者作为整体（如果您使用）提供的任何此类派生作品。复制和分发工作，否则遵循此许可证中所述的条件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-496">You may add Your own copyright statement to Your modifications and may provide additional or different license terms and conditions for use, reproduction, or distribution of Your modifications, or for any such Derivative Works as a whole, provided Your use, reproduction, and distribution of the Work otherwise complies with the conditions stated in this License.</span></span>

   5. <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-497">提交发布内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-497">Submission of Contributions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-498">除非明确说明，否则任何有意提交给许可方的作品中的任何发布都必须符合此许可证的条款和条件，不需要任何其他条款或条件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-498">Unless You explicitly state otherwise, any Contribution intentionally submitted for inclusion in the Work by You to the Licensor shall be under the terms and conditions of this License, without any additional terms or conditions.</span></span>
      <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-499">尽管如此，此处的任何内容都不应取代或修改您可能已在许可方中对此类发布执行的任何单独许可协议的条款。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-499">Notwithstanding the above, nothing herein shall supersede or modify the terms of any separate license agreement you may have executed with Licensor regarding such Contributions.</span></span>

   6. <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-500">商标.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-500">Trademarks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-501">此许可证不授予使用许可方的商业名称、商标、服务标记或产品名称的权限，除了描述工作的来源和复制通知文件的内容所需的合理和惯例之外。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-501">This License does not grant permission to use the trade names, trademarks, service marks, or product names of the Licensor, except as required for reasonable and customary use in describing the origin of the Work and reproducing the content of the NOTICE file.</span></span>

   7. <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-502">担保免责声明。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-502">Disclaimer of Warranty.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-503">除非适用法律要求或书面同意，否则许可方提供工作（且每个参与者都按 "原样" 提供自己的贡献），无需任何明示或暗示的担保或条件（包括但不限于）任何种类的任何形式（包括但不限于）标题、非侵权性、适销性或特定用途适用性的担保或条件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-503">Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, Licensor provides the Work (and each Contributor provides its Contributions) on an "AS IS" BASIS, WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied, including, without limitation, any warranties or conditions of TITLE, NON-INFRINGEMENT, MERCHANTABILITY, or FITNESS FOR A PARTICULAR PURPOSE.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-504">您将独自负责确定使用或重新分发工作的 appropriateness，并假定在此许可证下与您的权限相关的任何风险。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-504">You are solely responsible for determining the appropriateness of using or redistributing the Work and assume any risks associated with Your exercise of permissions under this License.</span></span>

   8. <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-505">责任限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-505">Limitation of Liability.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-506">无论适用法律的要求（如故意和 grossly negligent 行为）或书面同意，除非适用法律（如故意和行为）或书面同意，否则在任何情况下都不会在法律理论的情况下进行任何责任，否则，任何参与者都应对您造成损害承担责任。包含由于本许可证或使用不足或无法使用工作（包括但不限于商誉丢失、工作中断、计算机等损失）导致的任何字符的任何直接、间接、特殊、偶然或后果性的损坏。故障或故障，或任何和所有其他商业损坏或丢失，即使已告知此类损坏可能性的情况也是如此。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-506">In no event and under no legal theory, whether in tort (including negligence), contract, or otherwise, unless required by applicable law (such as deliberate and grossly negligent acts) or agreed to in writing, shall any Contributor be liable to You for damages, including any direct, indirect, special, incidental, or consequential damages of any character arising as a result of this License or out of the use or inability to use the Work (including but not limited to damages for loss of goodwill, work stoppage, computer failure or malfunction, or any and all other commercial damages or losses), even if such Contributor has been advised of the possibility of such damages.</span></span>

   9. <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-507">接受担保或其他责任。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-507">Accepting Warranty or Additional Liability.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-508">在重新发布工作或衍生作品的过程中，您可以选择在接受支持、保修、indemnity 或其他责任义务和/或权限与此许可证一致的同时收取费用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-508">While redistributing the Work or Derivative Works thereof, You may choose to offer, and charge a fee for, acceptance of support, warranty, indemnity, or other liability obligations and/or rights consistent with this License.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-509">但是，在接受此类义务时，您可以仅代表自己自己，并根据您自己的责任，而不是代表任何其他参与者，并且仅当您同意赔偿、保护和持有每个参与者因或声明导致的任何责任时无害的行为根据接受任何此类担保或其他责任的原因，对此类参与者进行声明。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-509">However, in accepting such obligations, You may act only on Your own behalf and on Your sole responsibility, not on behalf of any other Contributor, and only if You agree to indemnify, defend, and hold each Contributor harmless for any liability incurred by, or claims asserted against, such Contributor by reason of your accepting any such warranty or additional liability.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-510">条款和条件结束</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-510">END OF TERMS AND CONDITIONS</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-511">附录：如何将 Apache 许可证应用于您的工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-511">APPENDIX: How to apply the Apache License to your work.</span></span>

      <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-512">若要将 Apache 许可证应用于你的工作，请附加以下样板通知，并将括在括号{}中的字段替换为你自己的标识信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-512">To apply the Apache License to your work, attach the following boilerplate notice, with the fields enclosed by brackets "{}" replaced with your own identifying information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-513">（不要包含括号！） 文本应包含在文件格式的相应注释语法中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-513">(Don't include the brackets!)  The text should be enclosed in the appropriate comment syntax for the file format.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-514">我们还建议将文件或类名称和用途说明包含在与版权声明相同的 "打印页" 中，以便更易于在第三方存档中进行识别。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-514">We also recommend that a file or class name and description of purpose be included on the same "printed page" as the copyright notice for easier identification within third-party archives.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-563">使用、复制和分发的条款和条件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-563">TERMS AND CONDITIONS FOR USE, REPRODUCTION, AND DISTRIBUTION</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-564">限定.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-564">Definitions.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-565">"许可证" 是指本文档的第1和第9节所定义的使用、复制和分发的条款和条件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-565">"License" shall mean the terms and conditions for use, reproduction, and distribution as defined by Sections 1 through 9 of this document.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-566">"许可方" 是指由授予许可证的版权所有所有者授权的版权所有者或实体。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-566">"Licensor" shall mean the copyright owner or entity authorized by the copyright owner that is granting the License.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-567">"法人" 是指使用该实体的公共控制和控制、控制的作用图元和所有其他实体的联合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-567">"Legal Entity" shall mean the union of the acting entity and all other entities that control, are controlled by, or are under common control with that entity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-568">出于此定义的目的，"控制" 是指（i）电源、直接或间接地引发此类实体的方向或管理（无论是按合同还是以其他方式）或（ii）所有权的50% （50%）或（iii）对此类实体拥有有益所有权的多个未完成的共享或（iii）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-568">For the purposes of this definition, "control" means (i) the power, direct or indirect, to cause the direction or management of such entity, whether by contract or otherwise, or (ii) ownership of fifty percent (50%) or more of the outstanding shares, or (iii) beneficial ownership of such entity.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-569">"您" （或 "您的"）是指由该许可证授予的个人或法律实体的权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-569">"You" (or "Your") shall mean an individual or Legal Entity exercising permissions granted by this License.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-570">"源" 表单应表示进行修改的首选表单，包括但不限于软件源代码、文档源和配置文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-570">"Source" form shall mean the preferred form for making modifications, including but not limited to software source code, documentation source, and configuration files.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-571">"对象" 表单是指从机械转换或源表单转换中产生的任何表单，包括但不限于已编译的对象代码、生成的文档以及转换为其他媒体类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-571">"Object" form shall mean any form resulting from mechanical transformation or translation of a Source form, including but not limited to compiled object code, generated documentation, and conversions to other media types.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-572">"工时" 是指在许可证下提供的 authorship （在源表单或对象表单中）的工作，如中所包含或附加到工作中的版权声明所指示（以下附录中提供了示例）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-572">"Work" shall mean the work of authorship, whether in Source or Object form, made available under the License, as indicated by a copyright notice that is included in or attached to the work (an example is provided in the Appendix below).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-573">"衍生品" 是指在源或对象窗体中基于（或衍生自）工作，以及编辑修订、批注、elaborations 或其他修改都代表 authorship 的原始工作的任何工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-573">"Derivative Works" shall mean any work, whether in Source or Object form, that is based on (or derived from) the Work and for which the editorial revisions, annotations, elaborations, or other modifications represent, as a whole, an original work of authorship.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-574">出于此许可证的目的，衍生品不应包括可从其分离的工作，或者仅链接（或按名称绑定）到的接口，工作和衍生工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-574">For the purposes of this License, Derivative Works shall not include works that remain separable from, or merely link (or bind by name) to the interfaces of, the Work and Derivative Works thereof.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-575">"贡献" 是指 authorship 的任何工作，包括原始版本的工作，以及对该工作或衍生作品的任何修改或补充，这些都是有意提交到许可方以供版权所有者在工作中包含的，或者由授权在代表版权所有者提交的个人或法律实体。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-575">"Contribution" shall mean any work of authorship, including the original version of the Work and any modifications or additions to that Work or Derivative Works thereof, that is intentionally submitted to Licensor for inclusion in the Work by the copyright owner or by an individual or Legal Entity authorized to submit on behalf of the copyright owner.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-576">对于此定义，"已提交" 表示发送给许可方或其代表的任何形式的电子、口头或书面通信，包括但不限于电子邮件列表、源代码控制系统和颁发或代表的用于讨论和改进工作的许可方的跟踪系统，但不包括被 conspicuously 标记或指定为版权所有者写入的内容为 "不是投稿" 的通信。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-576">For the purposes of this definition, "submitted" means any form of electronic, verbal, or written communication sent to the Licensor or its representatives, including but not limited to communication on electronic mailing lists, source code control systems, and issue tracking systems that are managed by, or on behalf of, the Licensor for the purpose of discussing and improving the Work, but excluding communication that is conspicuously marked or otherwise designated in writing by the copyright owner as "Not a Contribution."</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-577">"投稿人" 是指许可方和任何个人或法人代表许可方接收到的内容，随后合并在工作中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-577">"Contributor" shall mean Licensor and any individual or Legal Entity on behalf of whom a Contribution has been received by Licensor and subsequently incorporated within the Work.</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-578">授予版权许可证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-578">Grant of Copyright License.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-579">根据此许可证的条款和条件，每个参与者特此授予您一种永久的、全球、非独占、免费、免版税、不可撤销的版权许可证，以重现、准备好的衍生作品、公开发布在源或对象窗体中执行、再颁发和分发工作以及此类派生作品。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-579">Subject to the terms and conditions of this License, each Contributor hereby grants to You a perpetual, worldwide, non-exclusive, no-charge, royalty-free, irrevocable copyright license to reproduce, prepare Derivative Works of, publicly display, publicly perform, sublicense, and distribute the Work and such Derivative Works in Source or Object form.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-618">此库根据 node.js MIT 许可证的`fs.realpath`条款`fs.realpathSync`在 node.js v 0.10 中绑定了和方法的一个版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-618">This library bundles a version of the `fs.realpath` and `fs.realpathSync` methods from Node.js v0.10 under the terms of the Node.js MIT license.</span></span>

## <a name="oauth-sign-v090"></a>[<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1047">oauth 签名 v 0.9。0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1047">oauth-sign v0.9.0</span></span>](https://github.com/request/oauth-sign/blob/master/LICENSE)

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1048">Apache 许可证</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1048">Apache License</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1049">版本2.0，1月2004</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1049">Version 2.0, January 2004</span></span>

http://www.apache.org/licenses/

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1050">使用、复制和分发的条款和条件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1050">TERMS AND CONDITIONS FOR USE, REPRODUCTION, AND DISTRIBUTION</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1051">限定.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1051">Definitions.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1052">"许可证" 是指本文档的第1和第9节所定义的使用、复制和分发的条款和条件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1052">"License" shall mean the terms and conditions for use, reproduction, and distribution as defined by Sections 1 through 9 of this document.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1053">"许可方" 是指由授予许可证的版权所有所有者授权的版权所有者或实体。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1053">"Licensor" shall mean the copyright owner or entity authorized by the copyright owner that is granting the License.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1054">"法人" 是指使用该实体的公共控制和控制、控制的作用图元和所有其他实体的联合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1054">"Legal Entity" shall mean the union of the acting entity and all other entities that control, are controlled by, or are under common control with that entity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1055">出于此定义的目的，"控制" 是指（i）电源、直接或间接地引发此类实体的方向或管理（无论是按合同还是以其他方式）或（ii）所有权的50% （50%）或（iii）对此类实体拥有有益所有权的多个未完成的共享或（iii）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1055">For the purposes of this definition, "control" means (i) the power, direct or indirect, to cause the direction or management of such entity, whether by contract or otherwise, or (ii) ownership of fifty percent (50%) or more of the outstanding shares, or (iii) beneficial ownership of such entity.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1056">"您" （或 "您的"）是指由该许可证授予的个人或法律实体的权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1056">"You" (or "Your") shall mean an individual or Legal Entity exercising permissions granted by this License.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1057">"源" 表单应表示进行修改的首选表单，包括但不限于软件源代码、文档源和配置文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1057">"Source" form shall mean the preferred form for making modifications, including but not limited to software source code, documentation source, and configuration files.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1058">"对象" 表单是指从机械转换或源表单转换中产生的任何表单，包括但不限于已编译的对象代码、生成的文档以及转换为其他媒体类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1058">"Object" form shall mean any form resulting from mechanical transformation or translation of a Source form, including but not limited to compiled object code, generated documentation, and conversions to other media types.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1059">"工时" 是指在许可证下提供的 authorship （在源表单或对象表单中）的工作，如中所包含或附加到工作中的版权声明所指示（以下附录中提供了示例）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1059">"Work" shall mean the work of authorship, whether in Source or Object form, made available under the License, as indicated by a copyright notice that is included in or attached to the work (an example is provided in the Appendix below).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1060">"衍生品" 是指在源或对象窗体中基于（或衍生自）工作，以及编辑修订、批注、elaborations 或其他修改都代表 authorship 的原始工作的任何工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1060">"Derivative Works" shall mean any work, whether in Source or Object form, that is based on (or derived from) the Work and for which the editorial revisions, annotations, elaborations, or other modifications represent, as a whole, an original work of authorship.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1061">出于此许可证的目的，衍生品不应包括可从其分离的工作，或者仅链接（或按名称绑定）到的接口，工作和衍生工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1061">For the purposes of this License, Derivative Works shall not include works that remain separable from, or merely link (or bind by name) to the interfaces of, the Work and Derivative Works thereof.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1062">"贡献" 是指 authorship 的任何工作，包括原始版本的工作，以及对该工作或衍生作品的任何修改或补充，这些都是有意提交到许可方以供版权所有者在工作中包含的，或者由授权在代表版权所有者提交的个人或法律实体。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1062">"Contribution" shall mean any work of authorship, including the original version of the Work and any modifications or additions to that Work or Derivative Works thereof, that is intentionally submitted to Licensor for inclusion in the Work by the copyright owner or by an individual or Legal Entity authorized to submit on behalf of the copyright owner.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1063">对于此定义，"已提交" 表示发送给许可方或其代表的任何形式的电子、口头或书面通信，包括但不限于电子邮件列表、源代码控制系统和颁发或代表的用于讨论和改进工作的许可方的跟踪系统，但不包括被 conspicuously 标记或指定为版权所有者写入的内容为 "不是投稿" 的通信。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1063">For the purposes of this definition, "submitted" means any form of electronic, verbal, or written communication sent to the Licensor or its representatives, including but not limited to communication on electronic mailing lists, source code control systems, and issue tracking systems that are managed by, or on behalf of, the Licensor for the purpose of discussing and improving the Work, but excluding communication that is conspicuously marked or otherwise designated in writing by the copyright owner as "Not a Contribution."</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1064">"投稿人" 是指许可方和任何个人或法人代表许可方接收到的内容，随后合并在工作中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1064">"Contributor" shall mean Licensor and any individual or Legal Entity on behalf of whom a Contribution has been received by Licensor and subsequently incorporated within the Work.</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1065">授予版权许可证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1065">Grant of Copyright License.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1066">根据此许可证的条款和条件，每个参与者特此授予您一种永久的、全球、非独占、免费、免版税、不可撤销的版权许可证，以重现、准备好的衍生作品、公开发布在源或对象窗体中执行、再颁发和分发工作以及此类派生作品。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1066">Subject to the terms and conditions of this License, each Contributor hereby grants to You a perpetual, worldwide, non-exclusive, no-charge, royalty-free, irrevocable copyright license to reproduce, prepare Derivative Works of, publicly display, publicly perform, sublicense, and distribute the Work and such Derivative Works in Source or Object form.</span></span>

3. <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1067">授予专利许可证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1067">Grant of Patent License.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1068">根据此许可证的条款和条件，每个参与者特此授予您一个永久的、全球性的、非独占的、免费、免版税、不可撤销的永久性许可证（除非本部分中所述）专利许可证进行制作、使用、提供销售、销售、导入并以其他方式传输工作，此类许可证仅适用于这些投稿人许可的那些专利声明，这些专利声明一定是由这些参与者提供的 infringed，也可以是其与此类工作的贡献的组合（s）。提交了 #a0 个内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1068">Subject to the terms and conditions of this License, each Contributor hereby grants to You a perpetual, worldwide, non-exclusive, no-charge, royalty-free, irrevocable (except as stated in this section) patent license to make, have made, use, offer to sell, sell, import, and otherwise transfer the Work, where such license applies only to those patent claims licensable by such Contributor that are necessarily infringed by their Contribution(s) alone or by combination of their Contribution(s) with the Work to which such Contribution(s) was submitted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1069">如果您对任何实体（包括跨声明或 lawsuit 中的 counterclaim）进行专利诉讼，宣称中加入的工作或贡献构成了直接或 contributory 的专利侵权行为，以及任何专利许可证根据此许可证向你授予此工作的许可证应在存档此类诉讼时终止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1069">If You institute patent litigation against any entity (including a cross-claim or counterclaim in a lawsuit) alleging that the Work or a Contribution incorporated within the Work constitutes direct or contributory patent infringement, then any patent licenses granted to You under this License for that Work shall terminate as of the date such litigation is filed.</span></span>

4. <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1070">重新.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1070">Redistribution.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1071">如果满足以下条件，则可以复制和分发任何媒体（无论是否有修改）中的工作或派生作品的副本。在源或对象窗体中，只要满足以下条件即可：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1071">You may reproduce and distribute copies of the Work or Derivative Works thereof in any medium, with or without modifications, and in Source or Object form, provided that You meet the following conditions:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1072">您必须为工作或衍生作品的任何其他收件人提供此许可证的副本;并</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1072">You must give any other recipients of the Work or Derivative Works a copy of this License; and</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1073">您必须让任何修改过的文件携带突出的声明，表明您已更改这些文件;并</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1073">You must cause any modified files to carry prominent notices stating that You changed the files; and</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1074">您必须在所分发的任何派生作品的源表单中，保留工作的所有版权、专利、商标和归属声明，不包括那些不与衍生作品的任何部分相关的声明;并</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1074">You must retain, in the Source form of any Derivative Works that You distribute, all copyright, patent, trademark, and attribution notices from the Source form of the Work, excluding those notices that do not pertain to any part of the Derivative Works; and</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1263">限定.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1263">Definitions.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1265">"许可方" 是指由授予许可证的版权所有所有者授权的版权所有者或实体。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1265">"Licensor" shall mean the copyright owner or entity authorized by the copyright owner that is granting the License.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1266">"法人" 是指使用该实体的公共控制和控制、控制的作用图元和所有其他实体的联合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1266">"Legal Entity" shall mean the union of the acting entity and all other entities that control, are controlled by, or are under common control with that entity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1267">出于此定义的目的，"控制" 是指（i）电源、直接或间接地引发此类实体的方向或管理（无论是按合同还是以其他方式）或（ii）所有权的50% （50%）或（iii）对此类实体拥有有益所有权的多个未完成的共享或（iii）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1267">For the purposes of this definition, "control" means (i) the power, direct or indirect, to cause the direction or management of such entity, whether by contract or otherwise, or (ii) ownership of fifty percent (50%) or more of the outstanding shares, or (iii) beneficial ownership of such entity.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1268">"您" （或 "您的"）是指由该许可证授予的个人或法律实体的权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1268">"You" (or "Your") shall mean an individual or Legal Entity exercising permissions granted by this License.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1269">"源" 表单应表示进行修改的首选表单，包括但不限于软件源代码、文档源和配置文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1269">"Source" form shall mean the preferred form for making modifications, including but not limited to software source code, documentation source, and configuration files.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1270">"对象" 表单是指从机械转换或源表单转换中产生的任何表单，包括但不限于已编译的对象代码、生成的文档以及转换为其他媒体类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1270">"Object" form shall mean any form resulting from mechanical transformation or translation of a Source form, including but not limited to compiled object code, generated documentation, and conversions to other media types.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1271">"工时" 是指在许可证下提供的 authorship （在源表单或对象表单中）的工作，如中所包含或附加到工作中的版权声明所指示（以下附录中提供了示例）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1271">"Work" shall mean the work of authorship, whether in Source or Object form, made available under the License, as indicated by a copyright notice that is included in or attached to the work (an example is provided in the Appendix below).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1272">"衍生品" 是指在源或对象窗体中基于（或衍生自）工作，以及编辑修订、批注、elaborations 或其他修改都代表 authorship 的原始工作的任何工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1272">"Derivative Works" shall mean any work, whether in Source or Object form, that is based on (or derived from) the Work and for which the editorial revisions, annotations, elaborations, or other modifications represent, as a whole, an original work of authorship.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1273">出于此许可证的目的，衍生品不应包括可从其分离的工作，或者仅链接（或按名称绑定）到的接口，工作和衍生工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1273">For the purposes of this License, Derivative Works shall not include works that remain separable from, or merely link (or bind by name) to the interfaces of, the Work and Derivative Works thereof.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1274">"贡献" 是指 authorship 的任何工作，包括原始版本的工作，以及对该工作或衍生作品的任何修改或补充，这些都是有意提交到许可方以供版权所有者在工作中包含的，或者由授权在代表版权所有者提交的个人或法律实体。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1274">"Contribution" shall mean any work of authorship, including the original version of the Work and any modifications or additions to that Work or Derivative Works thereof, that is intentionally submitted to Licensor for inclusion in the Work by the copyright owner or by an individual or Legal Entity authorized to submit on behalf of the copyright owner.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1275">对于此定义，"已提交" 表示发送给许可方或其代表的任何形式的电子、口头或书面通信，包括但不限于电子邮件列表、源代码控制系统和颁发或代表的用于讨论和改进工作的许可方的跟踪系统，但不包括被 conspicuously 标记或指定为版权所有者写入的内容为 "不是投稿" 的通信。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1275">For the purposes of this definition, "submitted" means any form of electronic, verbal, or written communication sent to the Licensor or its representatives, including but not limited to communication on electronic mailing lists, source code control systems, and issue tracking systems that are managed by, or on behalf of, the Licensor for the purpose of discussing and improving the Work, but excluding communication that is conspicuously marked or otherwise designated in writing by the copyright owner as "Not a Contribution."</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1276">"投稿人" 是指许可方和任何个人或法人代表许可方接收到的内容，随后合并在工作中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1276">"Contributor" shall mean Licensor and any individual or Legal Entity on behalf of whom a Contribution has been received by Licensor and subsequently incorporated within the Work.</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1277">授予版权许可证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1277">Grant of Copyright License.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1278">根据此许可证的条款和条件，每个参与者特此授予您一种永久的、全球、非独占、免费、免版税、不可撤销的版权许可证，以重现、准备好的衍生作品、公开发布在源或对象窗体中执行、再颁发和分发工作以及此类派生作品。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1278">Subject to the terms and conditions of this License, each Contributor hereby grants to You a perpetual, worldwide, non-exclusive, no-charge, royalty-free, irrevocable copyright license to reproduce, prepare Derivative Works of, publicly display, publicly perform, sublicense, and distribute the Work and such Derivative Works in Source or Object form.</span></span>

4. <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1282">重新.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1282">Redistribution.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1283">如果满足以下条件，则可以复制和分发任何媒体（无论是否有修改）中的工作或派生作品的副本。在源或对象窗体中，只要满足以下条件即可：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1283">You may reproduce and distribute copies of the Work or Derivative Works thereof in any medium, with or without modifications, and in Source or Object form, provided that You meet the following conditions:</span></span>

## <a name="tslib-v193"></a>[<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1505">tslib v 1.9。3</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1505">tslib v1.9.3</span></span>](https://github.com/microsoft/tslib/blob/master/LICENSE.txt)

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1506">Apache 许可证</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1506">Apache License</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1507">版本2.0，1月2004</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1507">Version 2.0, January 2004</span></span>

http://www.apache.org/licenses/ 

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1508">使用、复制和分发的条款和条件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1508">TERMS AND CONDITIONS FOR USE, REPRODUCTION, AND DISTRIBUTION</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1509">限定.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1509">Definitions.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1510">"许可证" 是指本文档的第1和第9节所定义的使用、复制和分发的条款和条件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1510">"License" shall mean the terms and conditions for use, reproduction, and distribution as defined by Sections 1 through 9 of this document.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1511">"许可方" 是指由授予许可证的版权所有所有者授权的版权所有者或实体。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1511">"Licensor" shall mean the copyright owner or entity authorized by the copyright owner that is granting the License.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1512">"法人" 是指使用该实体的公共控制和控制、控制的作用图元和所有其他实体的联合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1512">"Legal Entity" shall mean the union of the acting entity and all other entities that control, are controlled by, or are under common control with that entity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1513">出于此定义的目的，"控制" 是指（i）电源、直接或间接地引发此类实体的方向或管理（无论是按合同还是以其他方式）或（ii）所有权的50% （50%）或（iii）对此类实体拥有有益所有权的多个未完成的共享或（iii）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1513">For the purposes of this definition, "control" means (i) the power, direct or indirect, to cause the direction or management of such entity, whether by contract or otherwise, or (ii) ownership of fifty percent (50%) or more of the outstanding shares, or (iii) beneficial ownership of such entity.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1514">"您" （或 "您的"）是指由该许可证授予的个人或法律实体的权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1514">"You" (or "Your") shall mean an individual or Legal Entity exercising permissions granted by this License.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1515">"源" 表单应表示进行修改的首选表单，包括但不限于软件源代码、文档源和配置文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1515">"Source" form shall mean the preferred form for making modifications, including but not limited to software source code, documentation source, and configuration files.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1516">"对象" 表单是指从机械转换或源表单转换中产生的任何表单，包括但不限于已编译的对象代码、生成的文档以及转换为其他媒体类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1516">"Object" form shall mean any form resulting from mechanical transformation or translation of a Source form, including but not limited to compiled object code, generated documentation, and conversions to other media types.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1517">"工时" 是指在许可证下提供的 authorship （在源表单或对象表单中）的工作，如中所包含或附加到工作中的版权声明所指示（以下附录中提供了示例）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1517">"Work" shall mean the work of authorship, whether in Source or Object form, made available under the License, as indicated by a copyright notice that is included in or attached to the work (an example is provided in the Appendix below).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1518">"衍生品" 是指在源或对象窗体中基于（或衍生自）工作，以及编辑修订、批注、elaborations 或其他修改都代表 authorship 的原始工作的任何工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1518">"Derivative Works" shall mean any work, whether in Source or Object form, that is based on (or derived from) the Work and for which the editorial revisions, annotations, elaborations, or other modifications represent, as a whole, an original work of authorship.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1519">出于此许可证的目的，衍生品不应包括可从其分离的工作，或者仅链接（或按名称绑定）到的接口，工作和衍生工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1519">For the purposes of this License, Derivative Works shall not include works that remain separable from, or merely link (or bind by name) to the interfaces of, the Work and Derivative Works thereof.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1520">"贡献" 是指 authorship 的任何工作，包括原始版本的工作，以及对该工作或衍生作品的任何修改或补充，这些都是有意提交到许可方以供版权所有者在工作中包含的，或者由授权在代表版权所有者提交的个人或法律实体。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1520">"Contribution" shall mean any work of authorship, including the original version of the Work and any modifications or additions to that Work or Derivative Works thereof, that is intentionally submitted to Licensor for inclusion in the Work by the copyright owner or by an individual or Legal Entity authorized to submit on behalf of the copyright owner.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1521">对于此定义，"已提交" 表示发送给许可方或其代表的任何形式的电子、口头或书面通信，包括但不限于电子邮件列表、源代码控制系统和颁发或代表的用于讨论和改进工作的许可方的跟踪系统，但不包括被 conspicuously 标记或指定为版权所有者写入的内容为 "不是投稿" 的通信。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1521">For the purposes of this definition, "submitted" means any form of electronic, verbal, or written communication sent to the Licensor or its representatives, including but not limited to communication on electronic mailing lists, source code control systems, and issue tracking systems that are managed by, or on behalf of, the Licensor for the purpose of discussing and improving the Work, but excluding communication that is conspicuously marked or otherwise designated in writing by the copyright owner as "Not a Contribution."</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1522">"投稿人" 是指许可方和任何个人或法人代表许可方接收到的内容，随后合并在工作中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1522">"Contributor" shall mean Licensor and any individual or Legal Entity on behalf of whom a Contribution has been received by Licensor and subsequently incorporated within the Work.</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1523">授予版权许可证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1523">Grant of Copyright License.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1524">根据此许可证的条款和条件，每个参与者特此授予您一种永久的、全球、非独占、免费、免版税、不可撤销的版权许可证，以重现、准备好的衍生作品、公开发布在源或对象窗体中执行、再颁发和分发工作以及此类派生作品。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1524">Subject to the terms and conditions of this License, each Contributor hereby grants to You a perpetual, worldwide, non-exclusive, no-charge, royalty-free, irrevocable copyright license to reproduce, prepare Derivative Works of, publicly display, publicly perform, sublicense, and distribute the Work and such Derivative Works in Source or Object form.</span></span>

4. <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1528">重新.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1528">Redistribution.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1529">如果满足以下条件，则可以复制和分发任何媒体（无论是否有修改）中的工作或派生作品的副本。在源或对象窗体中，只要满足以下条件即可：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1529">You may reproduce and distribute copies of the Work or Derivative Works thereof in any medium, with or without modifications, and in Source or Object form, provided that You meet the following conditions:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1530">您必须为工作或衍生作品的任何其他收件人提供此许可证的副本;并</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1530">You must give any other recipients of the Work or Derivative Works a copy of this License; and</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1531">您必须让任何修改过的文件携带突出的声明，表明您已更改这些文件;并</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1531">You must cause any modified files to carry prominent notices stating that You changed the files; and</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1532">您必须在所分发的任何派生作品的源表单中，保留工作的所有版权、专利、商标和归属声明，不包括那些不与衍生作品的任何部分相关的声明;并</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1532">You must retain, in the Source form of any Derivative Works that You distribute, all copyright, patent, trademark, and attribution notices from the Source form of the Work, excluding those notices that do not pertain to any part of the Derivative Works; and</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1533">如果工作包含作为其分布的一部分的 "通知" 文本文件，则您分发的任何派生作品都必须包含此通知文件中包含的归属声明的可读副本，而不包括那些不属于任何部分的声明衍生品，至少在以下位置之一：在作为导数工作的一部分分发的通知文本文件中;在源表单或文档中，如果随衍生作品一起提供，则为或者，在导数的工作所生成的显示中，如果在通常显示此类第三方通知的任何位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1533">If the Work includes a "NOTICE" text file as part of its distribution, then any Derivative Works that You distribute must include a readable copy of the attribution notices contained within such NOTICE file, excluding those notices that do not pertain to any part of the Derivative Works, in at least one of the following places: within a NOTICE text file distributed as part of the Derivative Works; within the Source form or documentation, if provided along with the Derivative Works; or, within a display generated by the Derivative Works, if and wherever such third-party notices normally appear.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1534">通知文件的内容仅用于提供信息，不会修改许可证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1534">The contents of the NOTICE file are for informational purposes only and do not modify the License.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1535">您可以在所分发的派生作品中添加自己的归属声明，也可以在工作中添加声明文本的补充或作为说明，前提是无法将此类附加归属声明解释为修改许可证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1535">You may add Your own attribution notices within Derivative Works that You distribute, alongside or as an addendum to the NOTICE text from the Work, provided that such additional attribution notices cannot be construed as modifying the License.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1536">您可以向所做的修改中添加自己的版权声明，并提供其他或不同的许可条款和条件，以供使用、复制或分发所做的修改，或者作为整体（如果您使用）提供的任何此类派生作品。复制和分发工作，否则遵循此许可证中所述的条件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1536">You may add Your own copyright statement to Your modifications and may provide additional or different license terms and conditions for use, reproduction, or distribution of Your modifications, or for any such Derivative Works as a whole, provided Your use, reproduction, and distribution of the Work otherwise complies with the conditions stated in this License.</span></span>

5. <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1537">提交发布内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1537">Submission of Contributions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1538">除非明确说明，否则任何有意提交给许可方的作品中的任何发布都必须符合此许可证的条款和条件，不需要任何其他条款或条件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1538">Unless You explicitly state otherwise, any Contribution intentionally submitted for inclusion in the Work by You to the Licensor shall be under the terms and conditions of this License, without any additional terms or conditions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1539">尽管如此，此处的任何内容都不应取代或修改您可能已在许可方中对此类发布执行的任何单独许可协议的条款。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1539">Notwithstanding the above, nothing herein shall supersede or modify the terms of any separate license agreement you may have executed with Licensor regarding such Contributions.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1555">限定.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1555">Definitions.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1556">"许可证" 是指本文档的第1和第9节所定义的使用、复制和分发的条款和条件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1556">"License" shall mean the terms and conditions for use, reproduction, and distribution as defined by Sections 1 through 9 of this document.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1557">"许可方" 是指由授予许可证的版权所有所有者授权的版权所有者或实体。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1557">"Licensor" shall mean the copyright owner or entity authorized by the copyright owner that is granting the License.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1558">"法人" 是指使用该实体的公共控制和控制、控制的作用图元和所有其他实体的联合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1558">"Legal Entity" shall mean the union of the acting entity and all other entities that control, are controlled by, or are under common control with that entity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1559">出于此定义的目的，"控制" 是指（i）电源、直接或间接地引发此类实体的方向或管理（无论是按合同还是以其他方式）或（ii）所有权的50% （50%）或（iii）对此类实体拥有有益所有权的多个未完成的共享或（iii）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1559">For the purposes of this definition, "control" means (i) the power, direct or indirect, to cause the direction or management of such entity, whether by contract or otherwise, or (ii) ownership of fifty percent (50%) or more of the outstanding shares, or (iii) beneficial ownership of such entity.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1560">"您" （或 "您的"）是指由该许可证授予的个人或法律实体的权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1560">"You" (or "Your") shall mean an individual or Legal Entity exercising permissions granted by this License.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1561">"源" 表单应表示进行修改的首选表单，包括但不限于软件源代码、文档源和配置文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1561">"Source" form shall mean the preferred form for making modifications, including but not limited to software source code, documentation source, and configuration files.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1562">"对象" 表单是指从机械转换或源表单转换中产生的任何表单，包括但不限于已编译的对象代码、生成的文档以及转换为其他媒体类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1562">"Object" form shall mean any form resulting from mechanical transformation or translation of a Source form, including but not limited to compiled object code, generated documentation, and conversions to other media types.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1563">"工时" 是指在许可证下提供的 authorship （在源表单或对象表单中）的工作，如中所包含或附加到工作中的版权声明所指示（以下附录中提供了示例）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1563">"Work" shall mean the work of authorship, whether in Source or Object form, made available under the License, as indicated by a copyright notice that is included in or attached to the work (an example is provided in the Appendix below).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1564">"衍生品" 是指在源或对象窗体中基于（或衍生自）工作，以及编辑修订、批注、elaborations 或其他修改都代表 authorship 的原始工作的任何工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1564">"Derivative Works" shall mean any work, whether in Source or Object form, that is based on (or derived from) the Work and for which the editorial revisions, annotations, elaborations, or other modifications represent, as a whole, an original work of authorship.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1565">出于此许可证的目的，衍生品不应包括可从其分离的工作，或者仅链接（或按名称绑定）到的接口，工作和衍生工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1565">For the purposes of this License, Derivative Works shall not include works that remain separable from, or merely link (or bind by name) to the interfaces of, the Work and Derivative Works thereof.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1566">"贡献" 是指 authorship 的任何工作，包括原始版本的工作，以及对该工作或衍生作品的任何修改或补充，这些都是有意提交到许可方以供版权所有者在工作中包含的，或者由授权在代表版权所有者提交的个人或法律实体。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1566">"Contribution" shall mean any work of authorship, including the original version of the Work and any modifications or additions to that Work or Derivative Works thereof, that is intentionally submitted to Licensor for inclusion in the Work by the copyright owner or by an individual or Legal Entity authorized to submit on behalf of the copyright owner.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1567">对于此定义，"已提交" 表示发送给许可方或其代表的任何形式的电子、口头或书面通信，包括但不限于电子邮件列表、源代码控制系统和颁发或代表的用于讨论和改进工作的许可方的跟踪系统，但不包括被 conspicuously 标记或指定为版权所有者写入的内容为 "不是投稿" 的通信。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1567">For the purposes of this definition, "submitted" means any form of electronic, verbal, or written communication sent to the Licensor or its representatives, including but not limited to communication on electronic mailing lists, source code control systems, and issue tracking systems that are managed by, or on behalf of, the Licensor for the purpose of discussing and improving the Work, but excluding communication that is conspicuously marked or otherwise designated in writing by the copyright owner as "Not a Contribution."</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efc8d-1568">"投稿人" 是指许可方和任何个人或法人代表许可方接收到的内容，随后合并在工作中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efc8d-1568">"Contributor" shall mean Licensor and any individual or Legal Entity on behalf of whom a Contribution has been received by Licensor and subsequently incorporated within the Work.</span></span>
